(layout/style/ServoStyleSet.h, layout/style/ServoStyleSet.cpp): The primary entry point for style resolution. This class manages the set of style sheets that apply to a document, backed by a Servo Stylist. Key methods include StyleDocument() which performs a Servo traversal to compute style for all dirty nodes in the document, and ResolveStyleLazily() which resolves style for elements without assuming the style has been resolved.\\n\\n2. **ServoBindings** (layout/style/ServoBindings.h): Provides FFI (Foreign Function Interface) declarations for Gecko-to-Servo communication.
